May 21st Temple presents Zen Freeman \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n Since moving to Los Angeles in 2001, British DJ, producer, and remixer Zen Freeman has made a name for himself as the go-to DJ for high profile events around the world. Over the last 10 years, Zen has worked tirelessly perfecting his craft producing, scoring and sourcing music by day whilst playing clubs and events worldwide by night. His unwavering passion for discovering new music has allowed him to remain one step ahead of the curve, and his fans have taken notice  The mark of any great artist is the respect he is given by his peers - Zen is no different. His nearly telepathic ability to read a crowd has lead him to spin along with and for international superstars such as Paul Oakenfold, Black Eyed Peas, LMFAO, Nicki Minaj, Lady Gaga, Katy Perry, Justin Timberlake, Leona Lewis, Pete Tong, Felix Da Housecat, Moguai, Diplo, Vampire Weekend, The Black Key's, Jane's Addiction, Foster the People and Foo Fighters. His most recent remixes include collaborations with Paul Oakenfold, Brunette, Jump Jump Dance Dance, Remy Le Duc & EC Twins.  Zen has become a celebrity in his own right - his weekly residency for Perfecto at the 25,000 sq ft Rain Nightclub at the Palms Casino Resort in Las Vegas and his constant presence in the Hollywood club scene has generated buzz and allowed him to become the DJ of choice among top celebrities and A-list clientele. Some of his latest events include Elton Johns Oscar party, the Monaco Grand Prix after party, the Victorias Secret What is Sexy? party, Entertainment Tonight's EMMY after party, Harvey Weinsteins Golden Globe and Oscar after parties, Microsoft founder Paul Allens ultra exclusive Cannes Film Festival and St Barts New Years parties to name a few. He is also popular on the Film Festival circuit and plays every year at Sundance, Toronto and Cannes.  When Zen is not playing international high-profile events, he works as a music supervisor for major brands such as Prada, Soho House, Schrager Hotels and Weinstein Company.
